< Text>
Monday (Dec 10) the line was out into the entry room and stayed that way, even as 2 or 3 clerks continued to work - and the 2 automated clerk stations stayed busy.

The easy solution would be to have more clerks, but with an organization that is loosing billions of dollars, it's hard to hire more personnel.  And since the volume of first-class mail is down (albeit my Christmas cards single-handedly tried to remedy that problem, this year), their procedures suffer under the weight of the Christmas volume.

I'm thankful to have a post office - since folks in some places, some countries, don't have even this.<//Text>

When it came to the food the spaghetti and meatballs were absolutely to die for, especially the meatballs oh my goodness I want to go back and just buy meatballs tons of Meatballs.

Unfortunately that's where Pros kind of asked, the service was extremely slow. I don't know what was going on but it took forever for food to finally show up, the pizza showed up a couple of minutes after the appetizer so we really didn't get time to eat our appetizer. The mozzarella cheese sticks bread was lacking flavor, the cheese was good though. The pizza had very little cheese. I was fine with it being greasy and thin crust I love that, but the lack of cheese really took away from its taste. We ordered both the green beans and the broccoli and both were undercooked.

So in the end one out of the 5 things we ordered turned out to be really good. The other four dishes were average. The slow service especially bugged me because it wasn't a busy night. I don't know if they were understaffed or what was going on but it just annoyed the heck out of me and my associates

We spent quite a bit of $$$ on dinner and received no type of compensation nor apology.
The bottom line in our opinion is that Buca di beppo in Santa Clarita, vis-a-vis the inept manager, treats those with a physical disability (the wheelchair) as a nuisance rather than addressing the real issue, which was the rude and unruly children from the bigger party.
WARNING: people in wheelchairs or other disabilities might think twice before they choose Buca di Peppo for their dining experience.

P.S. Leisa our server was EXCELLENT and extremely professional.  She was very accommodating.  Bravo!<//Text>

< text>
I have always had a great meal at "Bucca di Beppo"! While the service has vacillated between very good and inattentive, the food has never disappointed. If you enjoy a celebration of Italy and Italian American culture, the interior decor and atmosphere is wonderful.

Two of my favorite highlights on the menu are the Chicken Marsala (the sauce!), and the Cheese Manicotti, which I consider the best I've ever tasted. The Fried Mozzarella (Antipasti) is also scrumptious!

Overall, you can't go wrong with "Bucca di Beppo". This is one of my favorite restaurants.<//text>
